from datetime import date, datetime
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler, MinMaxScaler
import torch.nn as nn

train_common = './data/common_dataprep/train.pickle'
test_common = './data/common_dataprep/test.pickle'

train_ganprep_noei = "./data/gan_dataprep/train_gan.pickle"
scaler_noei = './data/gan_dataprep/scaler.pickle'

train_ganinput_ei = 'data/gan_dataprep/train_ganinput_ei.pickle'

dtnow = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H')
output_generator = f'./data/generators/generator_{dtnow}.pt'
output_discriminator = f'./data/discriminators/discriminator_{dtnow}.pt'
output_loss = f'./data/losses/loss_{dtnow}.csv'



vars = [
    "VehPower", "VehAge", "DrivAge", "Density", "BonusMalus", "Exposure",

    "VehBrand", "VehGas", "Region", "Area",
"ClaimNb"]

             'VehBrand',
             'VehGas',
             'Region',
             'Area'
             ]

testsize = 0.2
valsize = 0.2

# Parameters
epochs = 15000
batch_size = 128 # Article: 128, Code: 1500 (not good)
disc_epochs = 2 # Both
gen_epochs = 1 # Both
loss_penalty = 1 # Article: 10, Code: 1
gen_bn_decay = .5 # Article: 0.9, Code: 0.25
disc_leaky_param = 0.2 # Both

learning_rate = 0.01 # Article: 0.01, Code: 0.001 (not good)
hiddens_gen = [100,100,100]
hiddens_disc = [55, 55]
round_with_beginning_set = -1

l2_regularization = 0.00001 # Article: 0, # Code: 0.1
gen_l2_regularization = l2_regularization
noise_size = 75 # z-size, Code: 100

Generator(
  (hidden_layers): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=75, out_features=100, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU()
    (2): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=100, bias=True)
    (3): BatchNorm1d(100, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.5, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (4): ReLU()
    (5): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=100, bias=True)
    (6): BatchNorm1d(100, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.5, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (7): ReLU()
  )
  (output): MultiCategorical(
    (output_layers): ModuleList(
      (0-13): 14 x Linear(in_features=100, out_features=1, bias=True)
      (14): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=11, bias=True)
      (15): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=2, bias=True)
      (16): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=22, bias=True)
      (17): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=6, bias=True)
      (18): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=5, bias=True)
    )
    (output_activations): ModuleList(
      (0-13): 14 x LeakyReLU(negative_slope=0.01)
      (14-18): 5 x CategoricalActivation()
    )
  )
)
Discriminator(
  (model): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=60, out_features=55, bias=True)
    (1): LeakyReLU(negative_slope=0.2)
    (2): Linear(in_features=55, out_features=55, bias=True)
    (3): LeakyReLU(negative_slope=0.2)
    (4): Linear(in_features=55, out_features=1, bias=True)
  )
)
